      <p>
       The potential energy depends on the velocity of the particle, so the force is velocity dependent, so it is not conservative.
      </p>
      <p>
       The relativistic Lagrangian is
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="mwe-math-element">
         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">

        </span>

      <p>
       The action is the relativistic
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Arclength" title="Arclength">
        arclength
       </a>
       of the path of the particle in
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_time" title="Space time">
        space time
       </a>
       , minus the potential energy contribution, plus an extra contribution which
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quantum_Mechanics" title="Quantum Mechanics">
        quantum mechanically
       </a>
       is an extra
       <a href="/wiki/Phase_(waves)" title="Phase (waves)">
        phase
       </a>
       a charged particle gets when it is moving along a vector potential.
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <table class="toccolours collapsible collapsed" style="text-align:left" width="80%">
         <tr>
          <th>
           Derivation of Lorentz force from relativistic Lagrangian (SI units)
          </th>
         </tr>
         <tr>
          <td>
           <p>
            The equations of motion derived by
            <a href="/wiki/Calculus_of_variations" title="Calculus of variations">
             extremizing
            </a>
            the action (see
            <a href="/wiki/Matrix_calculus" title="Matrix calculus">
             matrix calculus
            </a>
            for the notation):
           </p>

            <dd>
             <span class="mwe-math-element">
              <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
               <math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} \mathbf {P} }{\mathrm {d} t}}={\frac {\partial L}{\partial \mathbf {r} }}=q{\partial \mathbf {A}  \over \partial \mathbf {r} }\cdot {\dot {\mathbf {r} }}-q{\partial \phi  \over \partial \mathbf {r} }\,\!}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
                <semantics>
                 <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

                    <mfrac>

                   </mo>

                    <mfrac>
                     <mrow>
                      <mi mathvariant="normal">
                       ∂
                       <!-- ∂ -->
                      </mi>
                      <mi>

                      </mi>
                     </mrow>
                     <mrow>
                      <mi mathvariant="normal">

                      </mi>
                      <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

                   </mo>
                   <mi>

                   <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                    <mfrac>
                     <mrow>
                      <mi mathvariant="normal">
                       ∂
                       <!-- ∂ -->
                      </mi>
                      <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

                       </mi>
                      </mrow>
                     </mrow>
                     <mrow>
                      <mi mathvariant="normal">

                      </mi>

      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Relativistic_form_of_the_Lorentz_force">
        Relativistic form of the Lorentz force
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lorentz_force&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Relativistic form of the Lorentz force">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Covariant_form_of_the_Lorentz_force">
        Covariant form of the Lorentz force
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lorentz_force&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Covariant form of the Lorentz force">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <h4>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Field_tensor">
        Field tensor
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lorentz_force&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Field tensor">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h4>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main articles:
       <a href="/wiki/Covariant_formulation_of_classical_electromagnetism" title="Covariant formulation of classical electromagnetism">
        Covariant formulation of classical electromagnetism
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Mathematical_descriptions_of_the_electromagnetic_field" title="Mathematical descriptions of the electromagnetic field">
        Mathematical descriptions of the electromagnetic field
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Using the
       <a href="/wiki/Metric_signature" title="Metric signature">
        metric signature
       </a>
       <span class="nowrap">
        (1, −1, −1, −1)
       </span>
       , the Lorentz force for a charge
       <i>
        q
       </i>
       can be written in
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">
        <a href="#cite_note-33">
         [33]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <a href="/wiki/Lorentz_covariance" title="Lorentz covariance">
        covariant form
       </a>
       :
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <table cellpadding="5" style="border:2px solid #50C878;background: #ECFCF4; text-align: center;">
         <tr>
          <td>
           <p>
            <span class="mwe-math-element">
             <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
              <math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} p^{\alpha }}{\mathrm {d} \tau }}=qF^{\alpha \beta }U_{\beta }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
               <semantics>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                 <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                   <mfrac>
                    <mrow>
                     <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                      <mi mathvariant="normal">
                       d
                      </mi>
                     </mrow>
                     <msup>
                      <mi>
                       p
                      </mi>
                      <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                       <mi>
                        α
                        <!-- α -->
                       </mi>
                      </mrow>
                     </msup>
                    </mrow>
                    <mrow>

      <p>

      </p>

                 </mi>

              </mo>

                  <!-- Λ -->
                 </mi>
                 <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mi>

             </mstyle>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
             {\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} \mathbf {p} }{\mathrm {d} \tau }}=q\gamma \left(\mathbf {E} +\mathbf {v} \times \mathbf {B} \right)\,,}
            </annotation>
           </semantics>
          </math>
         </span>
         <img alt="{\frac {\mathrm {d} \mathbf {p} }{\mathrm {d} \tau }}=q\gamma \left(\mathbf {E} +\mathbf {v} \times \mathbf {B} \right)\,," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f6a5982dbab48c34170323abee65ee939b0a34b4" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:23.412ex; height:5.509ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       and since differentials in coordinate time
       <i>
        dt
       </i>
       and proper time
       <i>
        dτ
       </i>
       are related by the Lorentz factor,
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="mwe-math-element">
         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
          <math alttext="{\displaystyle dt=\gamma (v)d\tau \,,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
           <semantics>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
              <mi>
               d
              </mi>
              <mi>
               t
              </mi>
              <mo>
               =
              </mo>
              <mi>
               γ
               <!-- γ -->
              </mi>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               (
              </mo>
              <mi>
               v
              </mi>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               )
              </mo>
              <mi>
               d
              </mi>
              <mi>
               τ
               <!-- τ -->
              </mi>
              <mspace width="thinmathspace">
              </mspace>
              <mo>
               ,
              </mo>
             </mstyle>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
             {\displaystyle dt=\gamma (v)d\tau \,,}
            </annotation>
           </semantics>
          </math>
         </span>
         <img alt="dt=\gamma (v)d\tau \,," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/56f06acd0ba6d69c91dd899b8605b85d657e9388" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:12.805ex; height:2.843ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       so we arrive at
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="mwe-math-element">
         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
          <math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} \mathbf {p} }{\mathrm {d} t}}=q\left(\mathbf {E} +\mathbf {v} \times \mathbf {B} \right)\,.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
           <semantics>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mfrac>
                <mrow>
                 <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mi mathvariant="normal">
                   d
                  </mi>
                 </mrow>
                 <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mi mathvariant="bold">
                   p
                  </mi>
                 </mrow>
                </mrow>
                <mrow>
                 <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mi mathvariant="normal">
                   d
                  </mi>
                 </mrow>
                 <mi>
                  t
                 </mi>
                </mrow>
               </mfrac>
              </mrow>
              <mo>
               =
              </mo>
              <mi>
               q
              </mi>
              <mrow>
               <mo>
                (
               </mo>
               <mrow>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                 <mi mathvariant="bold">
                  E
                 </mi>
                </mrow>
                <mo>
                 +
                </mo>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                 <mi mathvariant="bold">
                  v
                 </mi>
                </mrow>
                <mo>
                 ×
                 <!-- × -->
                </mo>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                 <mi mathvariant="bold">
                  B
                 </mi>
                </mrow>
               </mrow>
               <mo>
                )
               </mo>
              </mrow>
              <mspace width="thinmathspace">
              </mspace>
              <mo>
               .
              </mo>
             </mstyle>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
             {\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} \mathbf {p} }{\mathrm {d} t}}=q\left(\mathbf {E} +\mathbf {v} \times \mathbf {B} \right)\,.}
            </annotation>
           </semantics>
          </math>
         </span>
         <img alt="{\frac {\mathrm {d} \mathbf {p} }{\mathrm {d} t}}=q\left(\mathbf {E} +\mathbf {v} \times \mathbf {B} \right)\,." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f21bbe37f9ca66094c61bd6e530c34cadc28adfd" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:22.149ex; height:5.509ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       This is precisely the Lorentz force law, however, it is important to note that
       <b>
        p
       </b>
       is the relativistic expression,
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="mwe-math-element">
         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
          <math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {p} =\gamma (v)m_{0}\mathbf {v} \,.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
           <semantics>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi mathvariant="bold">
                p
               </mi>
              </mrow>
              <mo>
               =
              </mo>
              <mi>
               γ
               <!-- γ -->
              </mi>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               (
              </mo>
              <mi>
               v
              </mi>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               )
              </mo>
              <msub>
               <mi>
                m
               </mi>
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>
                 0
                </mn>
               </mrow>
              </msub>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi mathvariant="bold">
                v
               </mi>
              </mrow>
              <mspace width="thinmathspace">
              </mspace>
              <mo>
               .
              </mo>
             </mstyle>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
             {\displaystyle \mathbf {p} =\gamma (v)m_{0}\mathbf {v} \,.}
            </annotation>
           </semantics>
          </math>
         </span>
         <img alt="\mathbf {p} =\gamma (v)m_{0}\mathbf {v} \,." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/556d59feefff54c4d8b325edf8ce3fc5ce455342" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:14.323ex; height:2.843ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <h3>
       <span id="Lorentz_force_in_spacetime_algebra_.28STA.29">
       </span>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lorentz_force_in_spacetime_algebra_(STA)">
        Lorentz force in spacetime algebra (STA)
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lorentz_force&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Lorentz force in spacetime algebra (STA)">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The electric and magnetic fields are
       <a href="/wiki/Classical_electromagnetism_and_special_relativity" title="Classical electromagnetism and special relativity">
        dependent on the velocity of an observer
       </a>
       , so the relativistic form of the Lorentz force law can best be exhibited starting from a coordinate-independent expression for the electromagnetic and magnetic fields
       <span class="mwe-math-element">
        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math alttext="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {F}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
             <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">
                F
               </mi>
              </mrow>
             </mrow>
            </mstyle>
           </mrow>
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle {\mathcal {F}}}
           </annotation>
          </semantics>
         </math>
        </span>
        <img alt="{\mathcal {F}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/205d4b91000d9dcf1a5bbabdfa6a8395fa60b676" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.927ex; height:2.176ex;"/>
       </span>
       , and an arbitrary time-direction,
       <span class="mwe-math-element">
        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math alttext="{\displaystyle \gamma _{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
             <msub>
              <mi>
               γ
               <!-- γ -->
              </mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mn>
                0
               </mn>
              </mrow>
             </msub>
            </mstyle>
           </mrow>
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle \gamma _{0}}
           </annotation>
          </semantics>
         </math>
        </span>
        <img alt="\gamma _{0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/407f2fbc64e21bb432f397fdb816de0f5083d900" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:2.259ex; height:2.176ex;"/>
       </span>
       . This can be settled through
       <a href="/wiki/Spacetime_algebra" title="Spacetime algebra">
        Space-Time Algebra
       </a>
       (or the geometric algebra of space-time), a type of Clifford's Algebra defined on a
       <a href="/wiki/Pseudo-Euclidean_space" title="Pseudo-Euclidean space">
        pseudo-Euclidean space
       </a>
       ,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">
        <a href="#cite_note-34">
         [34]
        </a>
       </sup>
       as
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="mwe-math-element">
         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
          <math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {E} =({\mathcal {F}}\cdot \gamma _{0})\gamma _{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
           <semantics>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi mathvariant="bold">
                E
               </mi>
              </mrow>
              <mo>
               =
              </mo>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               (
              </mo>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">
                 F
                </mi>
               </mrow>
              </mrow>
              <mo>
               ⋅
               <!-- ⋅ -->
              </mo>
              <msub>
               <mi>
                γ
                <!-- γ -->
               </mi>
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>
                 0
                </mn>
               </mrow>
              </msub>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               )
              </mo>
              <msub>
               <mi>
                γ
                <!-- γ -->
               </mi>
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>
                 0
                </mn>
               </mrow>
              </msub>
             </mstyle>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
             {\displaystyle \mathbf {E} =({\mathcal {F}}\cdot \gamma _{0})\gamma _{0}}
            </annotation>
           </semantics>
          </math>
         </span>
         <img alt="\mathbf {E} =({\mathcal {F}}\cdot \gamma _{0})\gamma _{0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ea7fd2c30633a5ab526e7e34411cb67cbb98e11a" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:14.787ex; height:2.843ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       and
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="mwe-math-element">
         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
          <math alttext="{\displaystyle i\mathbf {B} =({\mathcal {F}}\wedge \gamma _{0})\gamma _{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
           <semantics>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
              <mi>
               i
              </mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi mathvariant="bold">
                B
               </mi>
              </mrow>
              <mo>
               =
              </mo>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               (
              </mo>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">
                 F
                </mi>
               </mrow>
              </mrow>
              <mo>
               ∧
               <!-- ∧ -->
              </mo>
              <msub>
               <mi>
                γ
                <!-- γ -->
               </mi>
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>
                 0
                </mn>
               </mrow>
              </msub>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               )
              </mo>
              <msub>
               <mi>
                γ
                <!-- γ -->
               </mi>
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>
                 0
                </mn>
               </mrow>
              </msub>
             </mstyle>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
             {\displaystyle i\mathbf {B} =({\mathcal {F}}\wedge \gamma _{0})\gamma _{0}}
            </annotation>
           </semantics>
          </math>
         </span>
         <img alt="i\mathbf {B} =({\mathcal {F}}\wedge \gamma _{0})\gamma _{0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/90030cbe0db93ed3db9c8c2ae2847827307b280a" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:16.637ex; height:2.843ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       <span class="mwe-math-element">
        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math alttext="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {F}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
             <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">
                F
               </mi>
              </mrow>
             </mrow>
            </mstyle>
           </mrow>
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle {\mathcal {F}}}
           </annotation>
          </semantics>
         </math>
        </span>
        <img alt="{\mathcal {F}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/205d4b91000d9dcf1a5bbabdfa6a8395fa60b676" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.927ex; height:2.176ex;"/>
       </span>
       is a space-time bivector (an oriented plane segment, just like a vector is an oriented line segment), which has six degrees of freedom corresponding to boosts (rotations in space-time planes) and rotations (rotations in space-space planes). The dot product with the vector
       <span class="mwe-math-element">
        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math alttext="{\displaystyle \gamma _{0}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
             <msub>
              <mi>
               γ
               <!-- γ -->
              </mi>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mn>
                0
               </mn>
              </mrow>
             </msub>
            </mstyle>
           </mrow>
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle \gamma _{0}}
           </annotation>
          </semantics>
         </math>
        </span>
        <img alt="\gamma _{0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/407f2fbc64e21bb432f397fdb816de0f5083d900" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:2.259ex; height:2.176ex;"/>
       </span>
       pulls a vector (in the space algebra) from the translational part, while the wedge-product creates a trivector (in the space algebra) who is dual to a vector which is the usual magnetic field vector. The relativistic velocity is given by the (time-like) changes in a time-position vector
       <span class="mwe-math-element">
        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math alttext="{\displaystyle v={\dot {x}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
             <mi>
              v
             </mi>
             <mo>
              =
             </mo>
             <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mover>
                <mi>
                 x
                </mi>
                <mo>
                 ˙
                 <!-- ˙ -->
                </mo>
               </mover>
              </mrow>
             </mrow>
            </mstyle>
           </mrow>
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle v={\dot {x}}}
           </annotation>
          </semantics>
         </math>
        </span>
        <img alt="v={\dot {x}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/42318f114f153d55df03b96a8693b0247c1b3326" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.556ex; height:2.176ex;"/>
       </span>
       , where
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="mwe-math-element">
         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
          <math alttext="{\displaystyle v^{2}=1,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
           <semantics>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
              <msup>
               <mi>
                v
               </mi>
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>
                 2
                </mn>
               </mrow>
              </msup>
              <mo>
               =
              </mo>
              <mn>
               1
              </mn>
              <mo>
               ,
              </mo>
             </mstyle>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
             {\displaystyle v^{2}=1,}
            </annotation>
           </semantics>
          </math>
         </span>
         <img alt="v^{2}=1," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/34635a28904bd6fb795228872af1163cff72317d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:7.09ex; height:3.009ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       (which shows our choice for the metric) and the velocity is
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <span class="mwe-math-element">
         <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
          <math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {v} =cv\wedge \gamma _{0}/(v\cdot \gamma _{0}).}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
           <semantics>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
             <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mi mathvariant="bold">
                v
               </mi>
              </mrow>
              <mo>
               =
              </mo>
              <mi>
               c
              </mi>
              <mi>
               v
              </mi>
              <mo>
               ∧
               <!-- ∧ -->
              </mo>
              <msub>
               <mi>
                γ
                <!-- γ -->
               </mi>
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>
                 0
                </mn>
               </mrow>
              </msub>
              <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
               <mo>
                /
               </mo>
              </mrow>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               (
              </mo>
              <mi>
               v
              </mi>
              <mo>
               ⋅
               <!-- ⋅ -->
              </mo>
              <msub>
               <mi>
                γ
                <!-- γ -->
               </mi>
               <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                <mn>
                 0
                </mn>
               </mrow>
              </msub>
              <mo stretchy="false">
               )
              </mo>
              <mo>
               .
              </mo>
             </mstyle>
            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
             {\displaystyle \mathbf {v} =cv\wedge \gamma _{0}/(v\cdot \gamma _{0}).}
            </annotation>
           </semantics>
          </math>
         </span>
         <img alt="\mathbf {v} =cv\wedge \gamma _{0}/(v\cdot \gamma _{0})." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/898afe2e0045b1bfe8187de06f32c10af7e9497e" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:20.169ex; height:2.843ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       The proper (invariant is an inadequate term because no transformation has been defined) form of the Lorentz force law is simply
      </p>
      <dl>
       <dd>
        <table cellpadding="5" style="border:2px solid #50C878;background: #ECFCF4; text-align: center;">
         <tr>
          <td>
           <p>
            <span class="mwe-math-element">
             <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
              <math alttext="{\displaystyle F=q{\mathcal {F}}\cdot v}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
               <semantics>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                 <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
                  <mi>
                   F
                  </mi>
                  <mo>
                   =
                  </mo>
                  <mi>
                   q
                  </mi>
                  <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                   <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                    <mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">
                     F
                    </mi>
                   </mrow>
                  </mrow>
                  <mo>
                   ⋅
                   <!-- ⋅ -->
                  </mo>
                  <mi>
                   v
                  </mi>
                 </mstyle>
                </mrow>
                <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
                 {\displaystyle F=q{\mathcal {F}}\cdot v}
                </annotation>
               </semantics>
              </math>
             </span>
             <img alt="F=q{\mathcal {F}}\cdot v" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0d3416cf0c690a67efcc8edfae0e5ef6c6ae308b" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:10.642ex; height:2.509ex;"/>
            </span>
           </p>
          </td>
         </tr>
        </table>
       </dd>
      </dl>
      <p>
       Note that the order is important because between a bivector and a vector the dot product is anti-symmetric. Upon a space time split like one can obtain the velocity, and fields as above yielding the usual expression.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Lorentz_force_in_general_relativity">
        Lorentz force in general relativity
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lorentz_force&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Lorentz force in general relativity">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       In the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/General_theory_of_relativity" title="General theory of relativity">
        general theory of relativity
       </a>
       the equation of motion for a particle with mass
       <span class="mwe-math-element">
        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">

       </span>

       <span class="mwe-math-element">

       </span>

       <span class="mwe-math-element">

            </mrow>
            <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
             {\displaystyle m{\frac {Du_{c}}{ds}}=eF_{cb}u^{b}\;,}
            </annotation>
           </semantics>
          </math>
         </span>
         <img alt="{\displaystyle m{\frac {Du_{c}}{ds}}=eF_{cb}u^{b}\;,}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0d24804825f85cfc4a4eebf168a1ef34985a2f09" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:17.96ex; height:5.343ex;"/>
        </span>
       </dd>

      <p>
       where
       <span class="mwe-math-element">
        <span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;">
         <math alttext="{\displaystyle D}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
          <semantics>
           <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
             <mi>
              D
             </mi>
            </mstyle>
           </mrow>
           <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">
            {\displaystyle D}
           </annotation>
          </semantics>
         </math>
        </span>
        <img alt="D" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f34a0c600395e5d4345287e21fb26efd386990e6" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.924ex; height:2.176ex;"/>
       </span>
       is the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Covariant_differential" title="Covariant differential">
        covariant differential
       </a>
       in general relativity (metric, torsion-free).
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Applications">
        Applications
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Lorentz_force&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Applications">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <p>
       The Lorentz force occurs in many devices, including:
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Cyclotron" title="Cyclotron">
         Cyclotrons
        </a>
        and other circular path
        <a href="/wiki/Particle_accelerator" title="Particle accelerator">
         particle accelerators
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mass_spectrometer" title="Mass spectrometer">
         Mass spectrometers
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        Velocity Filters
       </li>
       <li>
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Magnetron" title="Magnetron">
         Magnetrons
        </a>
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Lorentz_force_velocimetry" title="Lorentz force velocimetry">
         Lorentz force velocimetry
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p>
       In its manifestation as the Laplace force on an electric current in a conductor, this force occurs in many devices including:
      </p>
      <div class="div-col columns column-count column-count-2" style="-moz-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2; column-count: 2;">
       <ul>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Electric_motor" title="Electric motor">
          Electric motors
         </a>
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Railgun" title="Railgun">
          Railguns
         </a>
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Linear_motor" title="Linear motor">
          Linear motors
         </a>
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Loudspeaker" title="Loudspeaker">
          Loudspeakers
         </a>
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Magnetoplasmadynamic_thruster" title="Magnetoplasmadynamic thruster">
          Magnetoplasmadynamic thrusters
         </a>
        </li>
        <li>
         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Electrical_generator" title="Electrical generator">
          Electrical generators
         </a>
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Homopolar_generator" title="Homopolar generator">
          Homopolar generators
         </a>
        </li>
        <li>
         <a href="/wiki/Linear_alternator" title="Linear alternator">
          Linear alternators
         </a>
        </li>
       </ul>
      </div>
